                     <div data-reactid="1603">
                      <div data-reactid="1604">
                       This darling 2 bedroom, 1 bath apartment is half a block from the beach and pier. French doors in the living room and dining room open onto the large sunny deck shaded by market umbrellas. The deck has a limited but lovely ocean view and is perfect for morning coffee, afternoon sun-tanning, and relaxing evening barbecues. Fully furnished with summery and comfortable colors and fabrics, this apartment sleeps six people (1 queen, 1 full, and 1 queen fold-out sofa in the living room).
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1605">
                       (Please see below about the special pricing.) There are 2 TV's, wifi, a full kitchen, lovely white tile in the bathroom, natural wood beam ceilings and refinished original oak floors. There is parking for 2 cars (one garage space and the driveway in front of it), and a coin-operated laundry in the building. Beach chairs, sand umbrella and boogey boards are provided for your convenience and seaside pleasure. Located in the heart of the popular Pier Bowl and blocks from San Clemente's historic downtown, this apartment is within walking distance of great restaurants, cute shops, the Sunday Farmers' Market and, of course, the beautiful beach.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1606">
                       San Clemente is a delightful little town, partly like Mayberry of tv fame, still a little like all lazy beach towns in California back in the day, and sort of like a destination resort with lots of great restaurants from the superb to the "it's-a-dive-but-I-love-it." This apartment is in the heart of the Pier Bowl. The Pier Bowl is the most popular beach neighborhood in San Clemente because of the wooden fishing pier, the great swimming and surfing beach, the lifeguard, and the convenient services for beachgoers. There are several delicious and fun restaurants just down the street from the apartment. There is a great coffee place so you can walk half a block in the morning, get a cup of coffee to go then walk across the street to watch the ocean change colors as the sun comes up and the seagulls pick up trash at the shoreline. One of life's great pleasures!
